  1458. # [10:38] <edmorley|sheriffduty> Gijs: re tbpl, the whole jobs disappearing thing is because {pending, running, completed} job data comes from three separate data sources, the first two loaded in the UI, the latter on the backend.   1459. # [10:38] <edmorley|sheriffduty> delay on the tbpl backend, then the ui polling the backend
